# ============================================================================
# CHAOS REDUX - EVENTS LOG SCRIPTED LOCALISATION
# ============================================================================
# Dedicated scripted localisation for events-log controls and history rows.
# Uses the filtered/sorted view arrays populated by rebuild_events_log_history_view.
# ============================================================================

defined_text = {
	name = GetEventsLogHistoryTypeView
	text = {
		trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				var = global.events_log_view_event_type_entries^events_log_history_index
				value = constant:event_system_event_type.major
				compare = equals
			}
		}
		localization_key = settings.major.colored
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				var = global.events_log_view_event_type_entries^events_log_history_index
				value = constant:event_system_event_type.repeatable
				compare = equals
			}
		}
		localization_key = settings.minor_repeatable.colored
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				var = global.events_log_view_event_type_entries^events_log_history_index
				value = constant:event_system_event_type.fire_once
				compare = equals
			}
		}
		localization_key = settings.minor_fire_once.colored
	}
	text = {
		trigger = { always = yes }
		localization_key = "Unknown"
	}
}

defined_text = {
	name = GetEventsLogFilterType
	text = {

	}
	text = {
		trigger = { check_variable = { settings_events_log_filter_type = 1 } }

	text = {

		trigger = { always = yes }

	}
}

defined_text = {
	name = GetEventsLogEventUniqueLabel
	text = {
		trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				var = global.events_log_events_view_unique_entries^events_log_history_index
				value = 0
				compare = greater_than
			}
		}
		localization_key = chaosx.events_log.events.unique.yes
	}
	text = {
		trigger = { always = yes }
		localization_key = chaosx.events_log.events.unique.no
	}
}

	text = {
		trigger = { has_global_flag = soviet_collapse_terminal_collapse }
		localization_key = chaosx.events_log.window.event_details.soviet_collapse.threat.terminal
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			SOV = {
				exists = yes
				check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat value = constant:soviet_collapse_super_event.union_unmade_high_threat compare = greater_than }
			}
		}
		localization_key = chaosx.events_log.window.event_details.soviet_collapse.threat.severe
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			SOV = {
				exists = yes
				check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat value = constant:soviet_collapse_super_event.union_unmade_contested_authority compare = greater_than }
			}
		}
		localization_key = chaosx.events_log.window.event_details.soviet_collapse.threat.rising
	}
	text = {
		trigger = { always = yes }
		localization_key = chaosx.events_log.window.event_details.soviet_collapse.threat.contained
	}
}
